Kids in kindergarten and primary school will benefit from GraphoGame’s evidence-based blended phonics and onset-rime teaching approach. \r\n\r\nDeveloped in collaboration with the University of Cambridge Centre for Neuroscience in Education, GraphoGame is the result of decades of research in dyslexia, neurolinguistics and neuropsychology. \r\n\r\nGraphoGame helps kids learn letters, rhymes and their sounds through a variety of engaging 3D levels – all with your child’s own unique player character! The player gradually moves on from graphemes and phonemes, through syllables and rhyme units, to eventually learn how to blend what they have learned into complete words.\r\n\r\nBy playing just 15 minutes regularly, kids can improve their letter knowledge, phonological awareness, reading speed and overall confidence in literacy!\r\n\r\nThe effectiveness of GraphoGame was studied in an efficacy trial funded by the Education Endowment Foundation and Wellcome Trust. To find out more, visit our website!\r\n\r\n\r\nFEATURES:\r\n\r\n• Evidence-based methodology \r\n\r\n• In-game literacy analytics for teachers\r\n\r\n• Child-friendly interface\r\n\r\n• Engaging 3D graphics\r\n\r\n• Character creation & customisation\r\n\r\n• Incentivised learning\r\n\r\n• Works offline \r\n\r\n• No advertisements\r\n\r\n• No in-app purchases\r\n\r\nNEW GRAPHOCLOUD ONLINE ACCOUNT\r\n\r\nPower-up GraphoGame with our new optional GraphoGame online account, GraphoCloud! \r\n\r\n• Now you can play with the same character on any device!\r\n\r\n• Save progress and research data on the cloud securely\r\n\r\n• Upload old players to your new GraphoCloud account\r\n\r\n• Create Groups that help categorise your players (for example, \"Classroom 1B\")\r\n\r\n• Share players with other GraphoCloud accounts and save player progress no matter where they play!\r\n\r\n\r\nTo register for a GraphoCloud account, go to the in-game logging screen at register!
